    function ReturnFromRequisitionItem() {
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup", "PurchaseRequisitionView", "PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView");
        var grid = $("#PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        if(grid != null)
            ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
    }

    $('#btnCopy__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");

        var prStatus = 'N';

        if (prStatus != 'N' &amp;&amp; prStatus != 'R' &amp;&amp; prStatus != 'S') {
            CopyRequisitionPopup(e);
        }
        else
        {
            if (prStatus == 'S' &amp;&amp; 'Admin Purchase Requisitions' == 'My Purchase Requisitions') {
                CopyRequisitionPopup(e);
            }
            else{
                SaveBeforeAnyOperation(e, "CopyRequisition")
            }
        }
    });

    function CopyRequisitionPopup(e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/CopyRequisitionPopup",
            data: { prId: '4030' },
                dataType: "json",
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success == true) {

                        var newPRID = result.NewPRID;
                        if (newPRID != null)
                        {
                            var aptaDataViewSelection;
                            var grid = $("#"+'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                            if(grid != null)
                            {
                                aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                            }
                            else{
                                aptaDataViewSelection = null;
                            }

                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup",data: {id : newPRID, origin:'PURCHASE_REQUISITION' , aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3' },type:"POST"});
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");

                        if(grid != null)
                            ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                    }

                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
            }
        });
    }

    $('#btnUndoSubmit__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");

    function UndoSubmiRequisitionPopup(e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/UndoSubmitRequisitionPopup",
            data: { prId: '4030' },
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success == true) {
                    var navigationID = 0;
                    if(AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView != null &amp;&amp; AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView != undefined &amp;&amp; AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView != '' )
                    {
                        var grid = $("#"+'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                        grid.dataSource.read();
                    }

                    if(!$('#btnSaveAndNext__PurchaseRequisitionView').is(":visible")){
                        navigationID = '4030';
                    }
                    else{
                        navigationID = '';
                    }

                    var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                    $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup",data: {id : navigationID, origin:'PURCHASE_REQUISITION' , aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3', adminPRApproverId: '' },type:"POST"});
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
            }
        });
    }

                    if(AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView != null &amp;&amp; AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView != undefined &amp;&amp; AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView != '' )
                    {
                        var grid = $("#"+'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                        grid.dataSource.read();
                    }
                    var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                    $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup",data: {id : '4030', origin:'PURCHASE_REQUISITION' , aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3', adminPRApproverId: '' },type:"POST"});
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
            }
        });
    }

    $('#btnApprove__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");

        var prStatus = 'N';

        if (prStatus != 'S') {
            ShowAjaxMessage('The requisition should be in submitted status to approve / disapprove.', "error","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
            return;
        }

        ValidateRequisitionBeforeApprove(e);
    });

    function ValidateRequisitionBeforeApprove(e) {

        var data = { prId: '4030' };

        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/ValidateRequisitionBeforeApprove",
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            data: data,
            success: function (result) {
                if (typeof result !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; result != null) {
                    if (result.Success == false) {
                        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup",data: {id : '', origin:'PURCHASE_REQUISITION' , aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3', adminPRApproverId: '', ValidateRequisitionBeforeApprove: true },type:"POST"});
                        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        SaveBeforeAnyOperation(e, "Approve");
                    }

                }
            }
        });
    }

    function ApproveRequisitionOnPopup(e) {
        var approverId = '';

        var selectedRowIds = '';
        var arr = selectedRowIds.split('~');

        var data = { approverId: approverId, approvalTrackingId: selectedRowIds, approvalType: '0' };

        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/RequisitionApproval/SingleRequisitionApproveAction",
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result.Success == 1) {
                    var navigationID = 0;

                    if(!$('#btnSaveAndNext__PurchaseRequisitionView').is(":visible")){
                        closRequisitionActiveWindow(e);
                        ShowAjaxMessage('Purchase Requisition approved successfully.', "success");
                    }
                    else{
                        navigationID = '';
                        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup",data: {id : navigationID, origin:'PURCHASE_REQUISITION' , aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3', adminPRApproverId: '' },type:"POST"});
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
                    }

                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function closRequisitionActiveWindow(e) {
        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow").close();
    }

    function DisapproveRequisitionOnPopup(e) {
        var approverId = '';

        var selectedRowIds = '';

        var data, options;

        data = { approverId: approverId, requireMyAttention: false, approvalTrackingId: selectedRowIds, approvalType: '0' , Ismultiple: false };
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/RequisitionApproval/DisapproveRequisition", data: data, type: "POST" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowDisapproveRequisition")
       .SetIsModal(true)
       .SetContent(options)
       .SetonClose(function () {
           if ($('#IsDisapprovedProcessed').val() == 1)
           {
               SaveBeforeAnyOperation(e, "Disapprove")
           }
       })
       .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
       .SetTitle('Disapprove Requisition')
       .SetWidth(550)
       .SetHeight(150)
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "RequisitionApproval", null);

    }

    function RefreshPopupAfterDisapproveRequisition(e) {

        var navigationID = 0;

        if(!$('#btnSaveAndNext__PurchaseRequisitionView').is(":visible")){
            closRequisitionActiveWindow(e);
            ShowAjaxMessage('Purchase Requisition Disapproved successfully.', "success");
        }
        else{
            navigationID = '';
            var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
            $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup",data: {id : navigationID, origin:'PURCHASE_REQUISITION' , aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3', adminPRApproverId: '' },type:"POST"});
            ShowAjaxMessage('Purchase Requisition Disapproved successfully.', "success","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
            UnRegisterActiveScreen();
        }

    }

    $('#btnDisapprove__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");

        var prStatus = 'N';

        if (prStatus != 'S') {
            ShowAjaxMessage('The requisition should be in submitted status to approve / disapprove.', "error","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
            return;
        }

        DisapproveRequisitionOnPopup(e);
    });
</script>

    function FixIE10Content() {
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content-wrapper").css("position", "");
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content").css("top", parseFloat(50) + "px");
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content").css("bottom", parseFloat(65) + "px");
    }
    $(document).ready(function () {
        var popUp = $(".FINSWindowcontainer").closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow");
        if (popUp !== undefined) {
            var browser = get_browser();
            if (browser.name == 'MSIE' &amp;&amp; (browser.version == 10)) {
                FixIE10Content();
            }
            else {
                $(".FINSWindowbody .content-wrapper").css("position", "relative");
            }
        }

    })

<script>
    function UpdateItemTotal() {
        var qty = $("#RequestQty").data('FINSUINumberInput').Value;
        var price = $("#PRUnitPrice").data('FINSUINumberInput').Value;
        if (qty &amp;&amp; price) {
            $("#ItemTotal").val((qty * price).toFixed(2));
        }
        else {
            $("#ItemTotal").val(null);
        }
    }

    function PurchaseRequisitionItemSave(saveNext, saveAdd, e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionItemDetailsPopup_Error");

        var errorMessage = '';
        if (errorMessage != '') {
            ShowAjaxMessage(errorMessage, "error", "PurchaseRequisitionItemDetailsPopup_Error");
            return;
        }

        var form = $("#RequisitionItemDetailsPopup");
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            url: form.attr('action'),
            data: form.serialize(),
            error: function (xhr, status, error) {
            },
            success: function (result) {
                if (result.Success == true) {

                    if (saveNext) {
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success", "PurchaseRequisitionItemDetailsPopup_Error");
                        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divPurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/ItemDetailsPopup", data: { PRId: '4030', prItemSequence: '', statusType: '3' , originPRItem: 'PURCHASE_REQUISITION', aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection } });
                        var grid = $("#PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                        grid.dataSource.read();
                        UnRegisterActiveScreen();

                    }
                    else if (saveAdd) {
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success", "PurchaseRequisitionItemDetailsPopup_Error");

                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/CreatePRItemPopup", data: { Id: '4030', statusType: '3', originPRItem: 'PURCHASE_REQUISITION' } });
                        var grid = $("#PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                        grid.dataSource.read();
                        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
                    }

                    else if ('1' &gt; 0) {
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow").close();
                        var grid = $("#PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                        if (grid !== null &amp;&amp; grid !== undefined) {
                            grid.dataSource.read();
                        }
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                    }
                    else {
                        var Id = result.Id;

                        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divPurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/ItemDetailsPopup", data: { PRId: '4030', prItemSequence: Id, statusType: '3', originPRItem: 'PURCHASE_REQUISITION' }, type: "POST" });

                        var grid = $("#PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                        if (grid !== null &amp;&amp; grid !== undefined) {
                            grid.dataSource.read();
                        }
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success", "PurchaseRequisitionItemDetailsPopup_Error");
                        UnRegisterActiveScreen();

                    }
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error", "PurchaseRequisitionItemDetailsPopup_Error");
                }
            }
        });

        GetPurchaseRequsitionTotalAmount();
    }

    $("#btnViewBudget__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var prItemID = '1';

        if (prItemID &lt;= 0) {
            ShowAjaxMessage('Please save Requisition Detail', "error", "PurchaseRequisitionItemDetailsPopup_Error");
            return;
        }

        var data = { prId: '4030' };
        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/GetViewBudgetData",
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result == "success") {

                    var grid = $("#PRViewBudgetDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    grid.dataSource.read();

                    $('#popupViewBudget').data("kendoWindow").center().open();
                    $('#popupViewBudget').data("kendoWindow").refresh();
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                }
            }
        });
    });

    function onRefreshpopupViewBudgetPopUp(e) {
        e.sender.title('View Budget');
        e.sender.center();
    }

    function closRequisitionItemWindow(e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionItemDetailsPopup_Error");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");

        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow").close();
        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
        GetPurchaseRequsitionTotalAmount();
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup", "PurchaseRequisitionView", "PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView");
    }

    $("#btnCancel__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        closRequisitionItemWindow(e);
    });

    $("#btnSaveAndNext__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        PurchaseRequisitionItemSave(true, false, e);
    })

    $("#btnSaveAndAdd__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        PurchaseRequisitionItemSave(false, true, e);
        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").SetTitle('Add Purchase Requisition Line Item');
    })

    $("#btnSave__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        PurchaseRequisitionItemSave(false, false, e);
        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").SetTitle('Edit Purchase Requisition Line Item');
    })
</script>

<script>
    function onRefreshAccountsPopup_PRItemDetails(e) {
        e.sender.title('Account Code Allocation');
        e.sender.center();

        setFocusEventForKendoWindow('popupMultipleAccountCodeGrid_' + 'PRItemDetails');
    }

    function onActivateAccountsPopup_PRItemDetails() {
        if ($("#tbAccountCodeEdit_" + 'PRItemDetails' + "acMultipleAccountCode").val() == '') {
            $("#tbAccountCodeEdit_" + 'PRItemDetails' + "acMultipleAccountCode").removeAttr("disabled");
        }
    }

    function onCloseRefreshAccountCode_PRItemDetails(e) {
        $("pupMultipleAccountCodeGrid_PRItemDetails").html('');
        var stagingId = $("#RequisitionStagingId").val()
        var data = { stagingId: stagingId };

        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/GetAccountCode",
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success == true) {
                    if (result.AccountCode) {
                        $.ajax({
                            cache: false,
                            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/AcAccountTextBox",
                            data: { AccountCode: result.AccountCode, AccountType: 'Expenditure', EnableAccountMask: 'True', Key: 'PRItemDetails' + 'acTextBox', AccountCodeWidthEm: "28", AllocationSequence: '0', AcAccountTextBoxOnChangeFunction: '' },
                            dataType: "html",
                            success: function (resp) {
                                $("#AccountCodeBox_PRItemDetailsacTextBox").html(resp);
                                if ('' !== '') {
                                    ;
                                }
                            }
                        });
                    }
                    //debugger;
                    $("#tbAccountCodeEdit_PRItemDetailsacTextBox").val(result.AccountCode);
                    if (result.AccountCode == "Multiple")
                        $("#tbAccountCodeEdit_PRItemDetailsacTextBox").select();
                }
            }
        });
    }
</script>

    <script>
        function btnOpenAccountCodeAssistant_PRItemDetailsacTextBox(e) {
            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowAccountCodeAssistant_PRItemDetailsacTextBox")
                .SetIsModal(true)
                .SetTitle("Account Code Assistant")
                .SetonActivate(function () { AccountCodeLookUpActivated_PRItemDetailsacTextBox(); })
                .SetonDeactivate(function () { ReturnFromAccountCodeLookup_PRItemDetailsacTextBox(); });

            finsWindow.CreateWindow(false).SetHTMLContent('&lt;div id="divACL_PRItemDetailsacTextBox" &gt;&lt;/div&gt;');
            onAccountCodeLookupWindowOpen_PRItemDetailsacTextBox();
            finsWindow.OpenWindow();
            e.preventDefault();
        }

        $(function () {
            $("#btnOpenAccountCodeAssistant_PRItemDetailsacTextBox").click(btnOpenAccountCodeAssistant_PRItemDetailsacTextBox);
        });

        function onAccountCodeLookupWindowOpen_PRItemDetailsacTextBox(e) {
            var accountType = $("#hdnAccountTypeAcAccountTextBox_PRItemDetailsacTextBox").val();
            //If an account type is selected in account code assistant popup, use that account type.
            if (!$("#tbAccountCodeEdit_PRItemDetailsacTextBox").val() &amp;&amp; $("#ACLAccountType_PRItemDetailsacTextBox").data("FINSComboBox") &amp;&amp; $("#ACLAccountType_PRItemDetailsacTextBox").data("FINSComboBox").Value) {
                accountType = $("#ACLAccountType_PRItemDetailsacTextBox").data("FINSComboBox").Value;
            }
            var data = {
                AccountType: accountType,
                Key: "PRItemDetailsacTextBox",
                AccountCode: $("#tbAccountCodeEdit_PRItemDetailsacTextBox").val()
            };

            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                async: false,
                url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/AccountCodeLookup",
                data: data,
                success: function (result) {
                    $("#divACL_PRItemDetailsacTextBox").html(result);
                },
                error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                    console.log(textStatus, errorThrown);
                }
            });
        }

        function AccountCodeLookUpActivated_PRItemDetailsacTextBox(e) {
            SelectedElementValues_PRItemDetailsacTextBox("tbAccountCodeEdit_" + 'PRItemDetailsacTextBox');
        }

        function ReturnFromAccountCodeLookup_PRItemDetailsacTextBox() {
            if (bOk) {
                bOk = false;
                var accountType
                var AccountId = $('#AccountId_PRItemDetailsacTextBox').data("kendoComboBox").value();

                if ($("#ACLAccountType_PRItemDetailsacTextBox").data("kendoComboBox") &amp;&amp; $("#ACLAccountType_PRItemDetailsacTextBox").data("FINSComboBox").Value) {
                    accountType = $("#ACLAccountType_PRItemDetailsacTextBox").data("FINSComboBox").Value;
                }
                else {
                    accountType = 'Expenditure';
                }
                $.ajax({
                    cache: false,
                    url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/AcAccountTextBox",
                    data: {
                        AccountCode: AccountId,
                        AccountType: accountType,
                        AccountCodeWidthEm: '28',
                        EnableAccountMask: 'True',
                        Key: 'PRItemDetailsacTextBox',
                        AcAccountTextBoxOnChangeFunction: '',
                        HtmlAttributeName: ''
                    },
                    dataType: "html",
                    success: function (resp) {
                        $("#AccountCodeBox_PRItemDetailsacTextBox").html(resp);
                        SetLabelDescriptionAccountCode('lblAccountDesc_PRItemDetailsacTextBox', AccountId);
                        if ('' !== '') {
                            ;
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
        }

<script>
    function AcMultipleAllocation_GetTotalAmount(unitsFN, unitPriceFN, amountFN, validate, precision) {
        var totalAmount = 0.0;

        if (amountFN != 'undefined' &amp;&amp; amountFN != '') {
            var amount = $("#" + amountFN).val();
            if (typeof amount != 'undefined') {
                if (validate &amp;&amp; (amount == '' || amount == '')) {
                    return null;
                }
                totalAmount = Number(amount);
            }
        }
        else {
            var orderQty = $("#" + unitsFN).val();
            var prUnitPrice = $("#" + unitPriceFN).val();
            if (typeof orderQty != 'undefined' &amp;&amp; (typeof prUnitPrice != 'undefined')) {
                if (validate &amp;&amp; (orderQty == '' || prUnitPrice == '' || orderQty == null || prUnitPrice == null)) {
                    return null;
                }
                totalAmount = Number(orderQty) * Number(prUnitPrice);
            }
        }

        return totalAmount.toFixed(precision);
    }

    function btnAccountcodeEditClick_PRItemDetails(e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        var key = 'PRItemDetails';
        var dv = 'MultipleAccountCodeDataView';
        var stgIdFN = 'RequisitionStagingId';
        var unitsFN = 'RequestQty';
        var unitPriceFN = 'PRUnitPrice';
        var amountFN = 'ItemTotal';
        var errFN = 'PurchaseRequisitionItemDetailsPopup_Error';
        var msg = 'Qty and Unit Price are required before Account allocation';
        var precision = 2;

        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", errFN);

        var accountCode = $('#tbAccountCodeEdit_' + key + 'acTextBox').val();
        var stagingId = $("#" + stgIdFN).val();
        var totalAmount = AcMultipleAllocation_GetTotalAmount(unitsFN, unitPriceFN, amountFN, true, precision);
        if (totalAmount == null || totalAmount == 'undefined') {
            ShowAjaxMessage(msg, "error", errFN);
            return;
        }

        var data = {
            accountCode: accountCode,
            stagingId: stagingId,
            Amount: totalAmount,
            dataview: dv,
            adjustAllocation: true,
                distributeStagingAmount: true,
            saveAllocationToUserSettings: true,
            acMultipleAccountCodeGrid: true,
            cycleId: '5'
        };
        var dataGrid = {
            DataView: 'MultipleAccountCodeDataView',
            AccountStagingId: '202200',
            Key: 'PRItemDetails',
            AmountFieldName: 'ItemTotal',
            TotalHoursFieldName: 'RequestQty',
            HourlyRateFieldName: 'PRUnitPrice',
            AccountStagingIdFieldName: 'RequisitionStagingId',
            AccountType: 'Expenditure',
            IsViewOnly: 'False',
            CycleId: '5'
        };

        var height = ('False' === 'False' ? 500 : 420);
        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/ProcessAccountCodeAllocation",
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success == true) {
                    var modelKey = 'PRItemDetails';
                    var accStagingId = (dataGrid.AccountStagingId == 0 ? (jQuery.isNumeric(result.StagingId) ? result.StagingId : 0) : dataGrid.AccountStagingId).toString();
                    dataGrid.AccountStagingId = accStagingId;
                    var w = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupMultipleAccountCodeGrid_" + modelKey)
                        .SetContent({
                            type: "POST",
                            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/AcMultipleAccountCodeGrid",
                            data: dataGrid
                        })
                        .SetIsModal(true)
                        .SetWidth(960)
                        .SetHeight(height)
                        .IsRetainHeight(false)
                        .SetTitle("Account Code Allocation")
                        .SetonActivate(function () { eval("onActivateAccountsPopup_" + modelKey + "()"); })
                        .SetonClose(function (e) { if (w.GetDialogResult() != 'Cancel') eval("onCloseRefreshAccountCode_" + modelKey + "()"); });

                    $("#" + stgIdFN).val(result.StagingId);
                    $("#hdnAccountStagingIdEdit_" + key).val(result.StagingId);
                    $("#hdnAccountStagingId_MultipleAccountCodeGrid_" + key).val(result.StagingId);
                    $('#tbAccountCodeGrid_' + key).val('');
                    $("#tbAmountGrid_" + key).val('');

                    RemoveTabRestrictiononPopup();
                    setFocusEventForKendoWindow('popupMultipleAccountCodeGrid_' + key);
                    w.CreateWindow(true);
                    RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, key, key);
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error", errFN);
                }
            }
        });
    }

    $(function () {

            $("#" + 'PurchaseRequisitionItemDetailsPopup_Error').html(message);
            $("#" + 'PurchaseRequisitionItemDetailsPopup_Error').addClass("global_message error");
        }
        else {
            ShowAjaxMessage(message, "error");
        }
    }

<script>

    $("#divPRViewBudgetDataView").data("AptaDataView")
        .SetFilterColumns('')
        .SetAutoLoad(false)
        .SetEditable(false)

    function LoadSettingsOnDemand__PRViewBudgetDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSettings__PRViewBudgetDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridSettings',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'PRViewBudgetDataView', GridHeight: '300', settings: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSettings__PRViewBudgetDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("Settings__PRViewBudgetDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand(dataViewKey) {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__" + dataViewKey).html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: dataViewKey, GridHeight: '300', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__' + dataViewKey).html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__" + dataViewKey + ": " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand__PRViewBudgetDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__PRViewBudgetDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'PRViewBudgetDataView', GridHeight: '300', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__PRViewBudgetDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__PRViewBudgetDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    $('#GridSettingsWnd__PRViewBudgetDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__PRViewBudgetDataView();
        $("#settingsWindow__PRViewBudgetDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();

        //refreshing source grid data
        var gridSource = $("#gridSettings__PRViewBudgetDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        gridSource.dataSource.read();

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetOtherGridSettingsOnLoad',
            cache: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'PRViewBudgetDataView' },
            success: function (result) {
                // debugger;
                if (result != null) {
                    // debugger;
                    var ddSortBy = $('#SortBy__PRViewBudgetDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortBy.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem.Text === result.SortBy;
                    });

                    var ddSortDir = $('#SortDir__PRViewBudgetDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortDir.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.SortDir;
                    });

                    var ddPageSize = $('#PageSize__PRViewBudgetDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");
                    ddPageSize.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.PageSize;
                    });
                }
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

    $('#SearchSettings__PRViewBudgetDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand__PRViewBudgetDataView();
        $('#tbFilterName__PRViewBudgetDataView').val("");
        $("#searchSettings__PRViewBudgetDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();
    });

    $('#ClearGridSettingsWnd__PRViewBudgetDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__PRViewBudgetDataView();
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/RestoreToDefault',
            cache: false,
            data: {
                gridName: 'PRViewBudgetDataView', GridHeight: '300', AutoAdjustHeight:
                          $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_PRViewBudgetDataView').val(),
                verticallyScrollable: 'True',
                selectedRecords: $("#PRViewBudgetDataView").data("kendoGrid").table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected"),
                isEditable: false
            },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#divPRViewBudgetDataView').html(result);
                InitializeGrid___PRViewBudgetDataView(false);
                var function_name = 'PRViewBudgetDataView__Restore';
                if (typeof (window[function_name]) === "function") {
                    window[function_name]();
                }

                var hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_PRViewBudgetDataView').val();
                if (hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal == "true") {
                    RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "PRViewBudgetDataView");
                }
                HideGridFooter("PRViewBudgetDataView", true);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

    $('#ExportToExcel__PRViewBudgetDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__PRViewBudgetDataView();
        $("#divPRViewBudgetDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExportToFile("XLS");
    });

    $('#ExportToPdf__PRViewBudgetDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__PRViewBudgetDataView();
        $("#divPRViewBudgetDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExportToFile("PDF");
    });

    $('#ClearSearchSettings__PRViewBudgetDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand__PRViewBudgetDataView()
        $("#divPRViewBudgetDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearFilterData();
        $('#divOptions__PRViewBudgetDataView').css("padding-top", "0px");
        $('#divQuickSearch__PRViewBudgetDataView').css("padding-top", "0px");
        $('#divQuickSearch__PRViewBudgetDataView').css("padding-left", "0px");
        $('#divOptions__PRViewBudgetDataView').css("margin-top", "0px");
        $('#divOptions__PRViewBudgetDataView').css("margin-right", "3px");
        $('#divQuickSearch__PRViewBudgetDataView').css("margin-top", "0px");
    });

    function MaintainGridState(grid) {
        MaintainGridStateHandler(grid, grid.element[0].id, '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveGridState');
    }

    function InitializeGrid___PRViewBudgetDataView(fromPageLoad) {
        var autoLoad = 'False' == 'True';
        //debugger;
        if ((fromPageLoad == true) || (!autoLoad)) {
            setTimeout(function () {
                GridGotoPage("PRViewBudgetDataView", "1");
            }, 300)
        }
    }

    function PersistGridSelectionOnPageChange(grid) {
        PersistGridSelectionOnPageChangeHandler(grid, this.element[0].id)
    }

    function grid_columnResize__PRViewBudgetDataView(e) {
        e.preventDefault = true;
        var grid = e.sender;
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function grid_columnReorder__PRViewBudgetDataView(e) {
        var grid = e.sender;
        e.preventDefault = true;
        grid.reorderColumn(e.newIndex, grid.columns[e.oldIndex]);
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function collapseGroupRows(grid) {
        grid.collapseGroup(grid.tbody.find("&gt;tr.k-grouping-row"));
        $('tr[role*="row"]').hide();
    }

    function PageLoad__PRViewBudgetDataView() {
        var gridName = 'PRViewBudgetDataView';
        var grid = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        //if its not gridsettings or gridsearchsettings
        if (gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsettings") == -1 || gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsearchsettings") == -1) {
            //
        }
        var hdnAutoAdjustHeight = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_PRViewBudgetDataView');

        if (parseBool("False")) {
            RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "PRViewBudgetDataView");
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('true');
        }
        else {
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('false');
        }

        var hdnScrollable = $('#hdnScrollable_PRViewBudgetDataView');
        hdnScrollable.val('true');
    }
    $(document).ready(function () { PageLoad__PRViewBudgetDataView(); });

    function grid_checkbox_onclick(fldName, gridName, theCheckBox) {
        var checked = theCheckBox.checked;
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theCheckBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            eval("dataItem." + fldName + " = checked");
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theCheckBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theCheckBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    function grid_textbox_onchange(fldName, gridName, theTextBox) {
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theTextBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theTextBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theTextBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    $('#UnselectAll__PRViewBudgetDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $("#divPRViewBudgetDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearGridSelection();
    });

    function FixIE10Content() {
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content-wrapper").css("position", "");
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content").css("top", parseFloat(50) + "px");
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content").css("bottom", parseFloat(65) + "px");
    }
    $(document).ready(function () {
        var popUp = $(".FINSWindowcontainer").closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow");
        if (popUp !== undefined) {
            var browser = get_browser();
            if (browser.name == 'MSIE' &amp;&amp; (browser.version == 10)) {
                FixIE10Content();
            }
            else {
                $(".FINSWindowbody .content-wrapper").css("position", "relative");
            }
        }

    })
